./commit-aec58cbd/staging/components/has/staging/kustomize.out.yaml: (object: application-service/application-service-controller-manager apps/v1, Kind=Deployment) object has 3 replicas but does not specify inter pod anti-affinity (check: no-anti-affinity, remediation: Specify anti-affinity in your pod specification to ensure that the orchestrator attempts to schedule replicas on different nodes.
